Competitive Programming.

Isaac Lozano Osorio

Solution to the problem.

Any questions do not hesitate to contact.


#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int main(){
    int N,C;
    // We can use dynamic programming to compute a solution
    bool *dp = new bool[10001+1]; // dp[N] = true -> P1 wins, else P2 wins
    while(scanf("%d%d",&N,&C)==2){
        if(N<=C && N!=1) { printf("%d\n",N-1); continue; }
        if(N==1) { printf("PIERDO\n"); continue; }
        dp[1]=false;
        for(int i=2; i<=C;i++){
            dp[i]=true;
        }
        bool flag;
        for(int i = C+1; i <= N; i++) {
            flag=true;
            for(int j=1; j<=C && N-j>=0;j++)
                if(dp[i-j] == false) { dp[i] = true; flag=false; break;}
            if(flag) dp[i] = false;
        }
        if(dp[N]) {
            int res = N;
            for(int i=N-1; i>=N-C && i>=0;i--){
                if(!dp[i]) { res-=i;  break; }
            }
            printf("%d\n",res);
        }
        else printf("PIERDO\n");
    }
    return 0;
}

//Other version
#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int main() {
    int n,k;
    while(scanf("%d%d",&n,&k)==2)
    {
        if((n-1)%(k+1)==0) cout<<"PIERDO\n";
        else cout<<(n-1)%(k+1)<<'\n';
    }
    return 0;
}
*/
